UGC · AIGC

6-1. Beijing Trend Consumers Aged 15–25

The 15–25 trend-consumer segment confirmed in Chaowai THE BOX membership data overlaps with SAGONG EE HO's primary persona by approximately 80%. This serves as direct grounds for adopting the Chaowai flagship as SAGONG EE HO's China debut stage.

6-2. Bilibili ACGN and VUP Fandom

As of Q3 2025, Bilibili reports MAU of 368 million, DAU of 113 million, and 25.4 million premium members. ACG content viewing time grew +25% year-on-year in Q2 2025. SAGONG EE HO's character IP and the MIMYO mascot can be exposed to a pool of 25.4 million premium members whose payment intent has been validated.

6-3. Douyin Short-drama Mass Audience

Douyin features a content environment with a micro-drama payment rate of 60% and a market size of USD 9.4 billion. More than half of viewers routinely pay per episode or pay to binge. SAGONG EE HO's 12-episode short drama enters this payment environment.

6-4. Xiaohongshu Lifestyle and Emotional Consumers

Xiaohongshu is a lifestyle platform whose user base is predominantly urban upper-middle-income women. SAGONG EE HO's goods, pop-up, and F&B collaboration lines connect directly with this platform's search and sharing behavior.

6-5. AI Creators and UGC Creator Pool

Within the 602 million generative AI users is a UGC creator pool that directly produces music, video, and characters. SAGONG EE HO's AI voice licensing, AIGC tool package, and UGC music composition channel within MAD BLOX are designed to connect with this pool.

6-6. Shared Code — Emotional Consumption

The shared emotional code running through the five personas is "the need to feel needed," "佛系," "摆烂," and "post-work emotional consumption." SAGONG EE HO's message — "It's okay to be different" — connects naturally with this emotional-consumption flow. SixthTone's description of Chiikawa's expansion in China as "character consumption that provides emotional comfort" illustrates the emotional demand that SAGONG EE HO's message can address.

Chapter 7

Five-IP Benchmark Matrix

POP MART × LABUBU · Miniso × Chiikawa · PLAVE · Hololive / VTuber · Restoration of the Korean Wave channel. We examine SAGONG EE HO's market position, growth ceiling, and entry path against five reference IPs.

7-1. POP MART × LABUBU

The POP MART × LABUBU case is a core benchmark that demonstrates the growth scale of China's character IP market. A single IP has already reached RMB 14.16 billion in annual revenue. The MIMYO blind-box line begins in a category that combines underdog sentiment, comfort-type characters, and unconventional appeal.

7-2. Miniso × Chiikawa Shanghai Pop-up

The Miniso × Chiikawa Shanghai pop-up generated RMB 2.7 million within 10 hours of opening and RMB 8 million in cumulative sales over three days, with on-site queues reaching 7,000 people as on-site demand concentrated very quickly (source: Yicai Global, 2024-04). The operational SOP for the SAGONG EE HO MIMYO pop-up uses the hourly sales and dwell-time data of the Chiikawa Shanghai case directly as its benchmark.

7-3. PLAVE (Virtual K-Pop Band)

PLAVE is a virtual K-Pop group whose February 2025 mini-album Caligo Pt.1 sold 1,030,000 copies in one week, becoming virtual K-Pop's first million-seller, and went on to sell out Gocheok Sky Dome. VLAST's 2024 revenue was KRW 45.4 billion (USD 32.5M), with an operating margin of 22% (source: Korea Times, 2025-11).

PLAVE is a major growth reference that SAGONG EE HO can study within the virtual K-Pop business. SAGONG EE HO sets OSMU expansion across the Korea, China, and broader Asia markets as its primary objective, and designs an entry path that combines character, music, goods, performance, and short drama.

7-4. Hololive / VTuber

Cover Corp (Hololive) recorded FY2025 revenue of ¥43.4B (approximately RMB 2.1B), with streaming revenue of ¥9.3B (+21.9% YoY). Annual SuperChat for top VTubers can reach USD 1M+. The Hololive model illustrates the upper bound of SAGONG EE HO's streaming, goods, fandom membership, and licensing revenue structure.

7-5. Restoration of the Korean Wave Channel — NetEase × JYP / HYBE → TME

In 2025 NetEase Cloud Music signed a licensing agreement with JYP Entertainment, securing the digital distribution rights for the JYP catalog in China (source: MBW, 2025). HYBE sold its entire stake in SM Entertainment to Tencent Music for USD 180 million. These are major signals that the Chinese music distribution infrastructure for Korean K-Pop is moving again.

SAGONG EE HO does not enter as K-Pop itself; rather, it is positioned as "a global character-music IP created by a Korean producer." This allows SAGONG EE HO to be designed as a structure that accounts for the Korea–China content distribution environment while leveraging trust in Korean production.

Chapter 8

C+C+C+X Business Structure Overview

Content · Community · Commerce · Exchange (trading and assetization). SAGONG EE HO is an execution structure capable of entering all four areas.

The business model of MAD POP AI Music Company is built around four core areas.

SAGONG EE HO is an execution structure that engages with all four of these areas. Chapters 9 through 12 detail the business cases SAGONG EE HO can build within each area.

Chapter 9 · A. Content

A. Content
SAGONG EE HO Content Roll-out

MAD POP's first signature character · full-pipeline digital music production · 30,000-artist management · idol IP incubation · international music education · copyright finance. SAGONG EE HO serves as the first execution case across six areas.

01
MAD POP's first signature character

SAGONG EE HO within MAD POP

A complete reference case of character, music, and worldview for the virtual idol and group customization features. A standard model that general users can refer to.

02
Full-pipeline digital production

Digital music content production

Composition, arrangement, recording, mixing, mastering, and OST — fully digitalized. Kim Hyung-suk's 25 years of K-Pop industrialization SOP applied directly. Three new tracks in Phase 1.

03
First execution of the 30,000-artist pool

Digital artist management

Structure that allows independent operation of each of the four characters. Demonstrates a dual track of AI digital singer and live-action content.

04
Group IP + digital rights of real members

Idol IP incubation

A combined group IP of a three-member band plus mascot. Direct linkage with the male-team and female-team group IP models. Digital rights of four members serve as assetized property.

05
One Person Studio standard case

International music education

Multi-region camp operation across Beijing, Seoul, and Asia. The combined model of four characters, worldview, music, and 11-channel OSMU serves as a case study.

06
SAGONG EE HO copyright registration

Copyright finance service

Integrated registration, rights confirmation, insurance, and revenue allocation across music, character, worldview, MV, and goods design. Data connects to the D axis (MAD EX).

9-1. ⓐ SAGONG EE HO within MAD POP — the First Signature Character

MAD POP is designed as a mass-market POP-making metaverse offering AI batch composition, choreography, 3D MV generation, virtual idol customization, and unified release across all platforms. SAGONG EE HO's four characters are an early reference case that demonstrates MAD POP's virtual idol and group customization features. They serve as a complete reference of character, music, and worldview that general users can consult when creating their own characters within MAD POP.

9-2. ⓑ Digital Music Content Production — Full-Pipeline Digital System

SAGONG EE HO's digital music operates through a full digital pipeline covering composition, lyrics, arrangement, recording, mixing, mastering, and OST. PDK Music Label's 25-year K-Pop industrialization SOP applies directly. Phase 1 releases three new tracks for the Chinese market along with mastered versions as a digital album, serving as an operational reference case for the digital music content production capability of the MAD POP platform.

9-3. ⓑ Digital Music Artist Management — First Execution of the 30,000-Artist Pool

The MAD POP business plan outlines a direction for expanding digital singer plus live singer management to a scale of 30,000 artists. SAGONG EE HO becomes the initial reference case for that operational system. The four characters — OREER.C (오리알씨), XOONY (쑤니), Itaewon Pak (One Pak), and MIMYO (미묘) — can each operate as independent characters, while demonstrating the dual track of AI digital singer and live-action content together.

9-4. ⓑ Idol IP Incubation — Group IP + Digital Rights of Real Members

SAGONG EE HO is a combined group IP of a three-member band and a mascot. This connects directly to the male-team and female-team group IP incubation models outlined in the MAD POP business plan. The character digital rights of the four members operate as assets within the IP incubation line.

9-5. ⓑ International Music Education — One Person Studio SAGONG EE HO Case

The MAD POP business plan presents the direction of building a One Person Studio talent system through multi-region education camps in Beijing, Seoul, and across Asia, and through collaboration with industry figures such as Kim Hyung-suk and Gong Jeong-hae. SAGONG EE HO serves as the standard case for this education line. The IP design model that combines four characters, a worldview, music, and 11-channel OSMU is a case study music creators can reference when designing their own IP.

9-6. ⓑ Copyright Finance Service Platform — SAGONG EE HO Copyright Registration

The financial service line integrating copyright registration, rights confirmation, insurance, and revenue allocation applies SAGONG EE HO's copyright registration as the priority case. Music, characters, worldview, MV, and goods design are all registration targets, and this data connects directly to the D axis (MAD EX).

9-7. Eight SAGONG EE HO Deliverables in the A Axis Phase 1 Content output list

The content SAGONG EE HO can deliver in Phase 1 within the A axis (Content) area is as follows.

Chapter 10 · B. Community

B. Community
The SAGONG EE HO World within MAD BLOX

MAD BLOX = a popular-music-centered UGC social game community benchmarked against Roblox. The SAGONG EE HO world = a Cabinet 402 virtual concert hall. A weekly metaverse live, plus UGC composition, MV, and avatar customization.

10-1. Definition of MAD BLOX

MAD BLOX is a popular-music-centered UGC social game community benchmarked against Roblox. It allows general users to create music-themed games and interactive scenes — music stages, concerts, dance rooms, idol training, and rhythm competitions — without coding.

10-2. The SAGONG EE HO World — Cabinet 402 Virtual Concert Hall

The SAGONG EE HO world is built as a virtual concert hall within the Cabinet 402 worldview. A weekly metaverse live is held on this stage, and fans can spend time on stage with the SAGONG EE HO members using their own avatars.

10-3. UGC Composition, MV, and Avatar Customization

Within MAD BLOX, a UGC environment lets general users use the SAGONG EE HO IP to create their own music, MVs, and avatars. By providing low-barrier tools, the SAGONG EE HO IP is designed to become not only material for consumption but also material for production.

10-4. Fan Creation Activation Policy

Fan-creation operating policies are designed with reference to the Luo Tianyi (낙천의) model. Fan-creation guidelines, copyright licensing rules, and reward structures for top creators are standardized. Cre8orClub's fandom and UGC operation know-how connects directly into this area.

10-5. Dwell-Time Structure

MAD POP provides a fast entry point into creation, and the SAGONG EE HO world within MAD BLOX provides a dwell structure where users can stay inside the character IP. As UGC composition, MV production, avatar customization, fan creation, and the weekly metaverse live accumulate, user dwell time lengthens, and the SAGONG EE HO IP expands from an IP for consuming content into a community-type IP where fandom resides.

Chapter 11 · C. Commerce

C. Commerce
SAGONG EE HO revenue lines
multi-axis expansion

AI XR concerts, the four concert scenarios, headlining the Yangguang Music Festival Series (阳光系列音乐节), touring through mainland China, Hong Kong, Macau, and Southeast Asia, F&B, convenience store, fashion, and beauty collaborations, MIMYO blind boxes, and Chiikawa-style pop-ups. Eight revenue lines are activated in Phase 1.

Weightings are design-stage estimates. They are calibrated against Phase 1 operating data.

11-1. AI XR Concerts — In-House Production and Release

SAGONG EE HO AI XR concerts are designed to be produced and staged at the Chaowai Flagship (朝外旗舰店) and then transmitted simultaneously through the secondary venue network. The core Commerce-line items in the MAD POP framework — digital music creation, XR concert production, full-channel release, and integration of MADverse global artist and concert resources — all apply to the SAGONG EE HO concert operation.

The MAD POP Commerce framework includes integrated operation of the music festival IPs under Master Gongtinghai and of the Yangguang Music Festival Series brand. SAGONG EE HO is an IP that can be proposed as a priority headlining candidate for the Yangguang series. This structure exposes the SAGONG EE HO IP directly to the existing Yangguang audience pool, and the collaboration track between producer Kim Hyung-suk and Master Gongtinghai provides a natural rationale for the headlining placement.

The MAD POP Commerce framework includes touring operations for the male and female teams across mainland China, Hong Kong/Macau, and Southeast Asia. The global business line of SAGONG EE HO IP Studio (led by VP Lee Seung-gyu) is integrated directly when the Southeast Asia sequence is initiated.

The CU, b;eat, E-Mart, and Seven Bräu track records held by SAGONG EE HO IP Studio are extended into industry-specific collaboration packages for the Chinese market. Five industry packages (convenience stores, F&B, fashion, beauty, and household goods) pre-designed by RATEL & PARTNERS as a 14-day execution package are activated in Phase 1. The detailed packages are organized in Appendix A11.

SAGONG EE HO × Seven Bräu BEER

This is a validated F&B collaboration track in the Korean market. 11-5b. Device and Consumer Electronics Collaboration — Samsung Galaxy Case Study

In the Korean market, the SAGONG EE HO IP ran a full collaboration with the Samsung Galaxy device lineup. Z Fold and Z Flip cases, Galaxy Watch bands and watch faces, and Galaxy Buds cases were produced on the basis of the four-character lineup and universe artwork. This case validates the IP integration potential with a leading Korean global manufacturer. In the Chinese market, it operates as the direct base for IP collaboration lines with the device divisions of Huawei, Xiaomi, OPPO, and vivo, with home appliance divisions, and with automotive brands such as BYD, NIO, and Xpeng.

11-6. Goods and Blind Boxes — MIMYO Line

Twelve MIMYO blind box SKUs, limited-edition goods, and pop-up-exclusive items are activated the fastest within the Commerce revenue lines. SKUs are designed with reference to the POP MART × LABUBU pricing structure (RMB 59–99 / limited editions RMB 200–1,000+).

11-7. Pop-ups and Themed Exhibitions — Applying the Chiikawa Shanghai Case

The hourly revenue and dwell-time data from the Chiikawa Shanghai pop-up are used as a direct benchmark to design the operating SOP for SAGONG EE HO pop-ups and themed exhibitions. Pop-ups and themed exhibitions at the Chaowai Flagship and across Tier 1–2 commercial districts are operated in parallel.

Chapter 12 · D. Exchange

D. Exchange
SAGONG EE HO IP asset structure

MAD EX is a music copyright and digital IP asset trading platform for the global POP music industry. Copyright registration, digital collectibles, music IP derivatives, IP rights packages, and the Hong Kong–Singapore dual track are designed as the four asset lines.

STEP 01

Copyright registration & rights confirmation

Music sources, characters, the universe, MVs, and goods designs are registered on the MAD EX primary copyright line.

STEP 02

Digital collectibles

Digital albums and MIMYO collectibles are released. Global expansion runs through the Hong Kong–Singapore dual track.

STEP 03

Music IP derivatives

Digital rights for the four characters and Cabinet 402 virtual stage assets are serialized and licensed.

STEP 04

IP rights packages

Copyrights, royalties, and IP commercialization rights are packaged into a standardized format. Long-term IP rights productization in Phase 2.

12-1. Definition of MAD EX

MAD EX is a music copyright and digital IP asset trading platform for the global POP music industry. It connects the confirmation, distribution, and financialization of music assets. After first establishing the systems for music copyright registration, copyright distribution, and licensing transactions, it supports trading of digital collectibles, digital albums, virtual stage assets, and music IP derivatives. Through its IP rights package framework, music copyrights, royalty income, and IP commercialization rights are bundled and designed into standardized asset products and financial transaction structures aligned with local regulation.

12-2. SAGONG EE HO Copyright Registration — Primary Entry into the D Axis

The copyrights for SAGONG EE HO music, characters, the universe, MVs, and goods designs are registered on the primary copyright line of MAD EX. This is the starting point that connects to the copyright finance service line described in Chapter 9, item A-6.

12-3. Digital Albums and MIMYO Digital Collectibles — Validated Issuance Record

The issuance of SAGONG EE HO digital album collectibles and MIMYO digital collectibles is under review. Given the digital asset regulatory environment in mainland China, the primary positioning of "copyright registration, distribution, and licensing" is maintained, while the Hong Kong–Singapore dual track secures the room for global expansion.

MIMYO-OFFICIAL · Genesis digital collectibles · Validated global issuance record

MIMYO — the track that validated the digital
asset potential of the SAGONG EE HO Universe

MIMYO is the Genesis digital collectible of the SAGONG EE HO Universe, issued into the global market. It was formally issued on the Ethereum mainnet contract and simultaneously listed on the world's #1 and #2 marketplaces, OpenSea and Element Market. 874 global holders hold 2,734 MIMYO collectibles, forming an actively trading community, and five full channels — Discord, Medium, X, YouTube, and Telegram — operate continuously. This is a track record in which the SAGONG EE HO IP has commercialized its music and character assets as digital assets in the global market, and it operates as the core base asset for the future SAGONG EE HO Universe digital collectible lineup.

→ For mainland China, it is repositioned within the digital collectibles category aligned with local regulation. The Hong Kong–Singapore dual track is a structure that directly leverages MIMYO's global issuance record and holder base. OpenSea MIMYO-OFFICIAL · Element Market

12-4. Music IP Derivatives — Character Asset Productization

The digital rights for the four SAGONG EE HO characters (OREER.C, XOONY, Itaewon Pak, MIMYO) are assets tradable in the form of music IP derivatives. Character design serialization and licensing of virtual stage assets (Cabinet 402 stage designs) are reviewed in parallel.

12-5. IP Rights Packages — SAGONG EE HO Long-Term IP Rights Structure

SAGONG EE HO music copyrights, royalty income, and IP commercialization rights are standardized and designed as long-term IP rights packages on MAD EX. The 11 channel revenue lines of SAGONG EE HO form a structure better suited to standardization and securitization than a simple music IP. This package is separated into the long-term IP rights productization domain after Phase 2.

12-6. Hong Kong–Singapore Dual Track

The Hong Kong–Singapore dual track is an alternative model designed with the mainland Chinese regulatory environment in mind. It is structured so that the SAGONG EE HO IP can be commercialized in both mainland and overseas markets.

The Badaling Campus is a base for education, accommodation, and practical training. The internationalized music education line referenced in Chapter 9, item A-5, operates from this base.

Chapter 15

MAD BLOX

16-1. Primary venue — flagship main-hall full set

At the 4,000㎡ Chaowai Flagship (朝外旗舰店) main hall, the SAGONG EE HO XR hologram full set is operated. A full-lineup stage featuring all four characters — OREER.C (오리알씨), XOONY (쑤니), Itaewon Pak (이태원팍), and MIMYO (미묘) — is the standard. Both the D+30 debut stage and the D+90 XR concert main run are staged at the primary venue. The stage design translates the Cabinet 402 worldview into stage architecture.

16-2. Secondary venue — 10,000+ synchronized broadcast SOP

SAGONG EE HO performances are simultaneously broadcast across more than 10,000 theaters, bars, hotels, shopping centers, and commercial real-estate sites. The licensing model is designed in the range of RMB 30,000–150,000 per session, exposing the SAGONG EE HO D+30 debut stage and the D+90 XR concert main run nationwide within the same time slot. Limited-edition MIMYO merchandise is sold at each synchronized venue to diversify revenue lines.

16-3. Large-scale IP immersive resident shows — Cabinet 402 resident space

A SAGONG EE HO Cabinet 402 resident space is operated within the Chaowai Flagship. Four to six themed exhibition channels run alongside the MIMYO line's merchandise, blind boxes, and AR experiences. It serves as the long-term operating base of the SAGONG EE HO IP, and from Phase 2 onward, resident-space expansion for new IP cards is under design.

16-4. High-frequency digital concerts — SAGONG EE HO World metaverse live

A weekly metaverse live is staged in the SAGONG EE HO World within MAD BLOX. Regular live shows accumulate fandom dwell time and payment frequency. This content is driven directly within the Community domain of the C+C+C+X model and connects directly to the Chapter 10 SAGONG EE HO World operation.

The SAGONG EE HO IP Studio Structure
An Integrated Execution Organization Operating the 402 IP

The SAGONG EE HO IP Studio is an integrated IP Studio that combines IP ownership, music production, global business, virtual and AI collaboration, data and branding, and creator community operations to carry out IP planning, production, distribution, marketing, and community operations together.

Chapter 17

SAGONG EE HO IP Studio Operating Organization

Kim Hyung-suk with Friends (Korea IP SPV) — under which NONUNI Raiders Entertainment · PDK Music Label · RATEL & PARTNERS · Cre8orClub form the four lines plus VP Lee Seung-gyu (NONUNI Raiders Entertainment, Global Business Lead) at the IP-company level execution organization.

17-1. Kim Hyung-suk with Friends (Korea IP SPV)

The Korea-side vehicle. Built around the SAGONG EE HO IP rights held by NONUNI Raiders Entertainment, it consolidates four lines — PDK Music Label, RATEL & PARTNERS, and Cre8orClub — into a single Korea-side IP operating entity. The interface with MADverse is unified at this SPV, which manages rights, contracts, settlement, and licensing under one roof. The global business strategy is led in-house directly by VP Lee Seung-gyu (see 17-6).

17-2. NONUNI Raiders Entertainment — Core IP Holder + Character Design / VFX line

NONUNI Raiders Entertainment is the rights holder of the SAGONG EE HO IP and simultaneously serves as the character design and VFX production line. Owning the 402 Diproma Universe worldview and the four-character IPs, it directly handles visual identity, design style guide, VFX, and real-time character visual operations.

17-3. PDK Music Label

PDK Music Label holds more than 25 years of production know-how covering the full K-Pop production pipeline — composition, arrangement, production, mixing, and live staging. Core assets include the catalog of works by Kim Kwang-seok, Kim Gun-mo, Park Jin-young, Solid, and Lim Chang-jung, and producer Kim Hyung-suk's personal network reaching into Korea's top-four agencies and the talent pool of writers, performers, session players, and directors.

17-4. RATEL & PARTNERS

RATEL & PARTNERS is responsible for data analysis, research, planning, marketing, branding, and business strategy. Market analysis, campaign design, brand building, performance operations, business development, overseas partnerships, and platform strategy are integrated directly into SAGONG EE HO operations. The Phase 1 per-channel KPI dashboards, persona matching reports, and brand collaboration packages are produced by RATEL & PARTNERS.

17-5. Cre8orClub

Cre8orClub leads the creator community and IP licensing operating line. It supports fandom building, UGC activation, creator collaboration, and IP licensing operations. The activation of fan creation within the SAGONG EE HO World, creator collaboration packages, and licensing operating plans are designed at Cre8orClub.

17-6. VP Lee Seung-gyu — NONUNI Raiders Entertainment global business strategy lead

VP Lee Seung-gyu is the strategist who scaled the global business of Baby Shark (Pinkfong) and SmartStudy. As an executive of Nonuni Raiders, he leads in-house, directly, the global IP asset development of SAGONG EE HO, market entry into the United States, Southeast Asia, and China, and the design of licensing business models. The Baby Shark IP is a representative K-IP case that started in Korea and grew global revenue and asset value. The operating assets from this case apply directly to the SAGONG EE HO global business.

17-7. Positioning

The 402 IP Studio is an execution organization at the level of an IP company that combines IP ownership, music production, global business, virtual technology, data and branding strategy, and creator community operations. SAGONG EE HO is operated under an IP Studio model that integrates four lines — NONUNI Raiders Entertainment (Core IP Holder + Character Design / VFX), PDK Music Label, RATEL & PARTNERS, and Cre8orClub — within Kim Hyung-suk with Friends (Korea IP SPV), with global business led by VP Lee Seung-gyu.

18-1. SAGONG EE HO IP ownership

The four characters — OREER.C, XOONY, Itaewon Pak, and MIMYO — the Diproma Universe worldview, the Cabinet 402 device, and the existing release catalog (WAKE UP, Polaris, Paper Plane, CIRCUS DA, and others) constitute the core IP assets held by the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio. They are owned by Nonuni Raiders Entertainment.

18-2. Kim Hyung-suk master catalog

The K-Pop catalog spanning 25 years — including Kim Kwang-seok, Kim Gun-mo, Park Jin-young, Solid, and Lim Chang-jung — is a music asset held by PDK Music Label. The method applies directly to SAGONG EE HO new-track production.

18-3. K-Pop industrialized production SOP

The Korean-style method for the full pipeline of composition, arrangement, production, mixing, and live staging is an industrialized SOP refined by PDK Music Label over 25 years. It is used as a standard case in the music education line of the joint operation.

18-4. Broadcast and media validation track

Experience with mainstream Korean media — including the first metaverse appearance on SBS Inkigayo on 2022-06-12 — is an asset. It is the basis on which SAGONG EE HO can enter the Chinese market with a history of being "a virtual IP validated within the mainstream music industry."

18-6. Korean brand collaboration track record

Character collaboration tracks validated in the Korean market — CU (convenience stores), b;eat (robot cafés), E-Mart (retail), and Seven Bräu (beer). They are used directly as case studies when designing industry-specific collaboration packages.

18-7. RATEL & PARTNERS data, branding, and business strategy assets

Proprietary market data, research methodology, brand-building SOP, performance campaign operating infrastructure, and business development and platform strategy know-how. The SAGONG EE HO per-channel KPI dashboards, persona matching reports, and brand collaboration packages are produced through these assets.

18-8. Cre8orClub creator community assets

A creator pool, fandom building know-how, UGC activation SOP, and an IP licensing operating system. The activation of fan creation within the SAGONG EE HO World and the IP licensing package are driven by these assets.

18-9. Nonuni Raiders global business strategy assets (VP Lee Seung-gyu)

An important asset is that an executive who actually grew the global market entry, licensing, and content IP asset development of Baby Shark (Pinkfong) and SmartStudy now leads the SAGONG EE HO global business directly from within Nonuni Raiders. These are the operating assets for the global revenue and asset-value expansion of K-IP.

18-10. 402 IP Bible

An IP operating document containing character settings, the worldview, narrative, tone and manner, and expansion rules. In Phase 1, it is converted into a Chinese-language IP Bible and used as the content quality standard for the joint operation.

18-11. Producer Kim Hyung-suk's authenticity authority base

Authority assets within the music industry, including Oxford ASMES Global Artist in Residence and candidate for the 25th presidency of the Korea Music Copyright Association. They are used directly when presenting the SAGONG EE HO IP to the market and media not as "character + music" but as "a character IP designed on top of an authentic music-industry method."

18-12. Domestic music and entertainment network

Producer Kim Hyung-suk's personal network, reaching into Korea's top-four agencies and the talent pool of writers, performers, session players, and directors, functions as a direct collaboration line for SAGONG EE HO new-track, MV, XR concert, and live performance production.

Three MVs corresponding to the three new tracks, and one live performance at the Chinese debut main hall, are the first deliverables. A first staging plan for the hologram and live-action stages is provided together.

19-4. 12 MIMYO blind-box SKUs

A first design of 12 blind-box designs using the MIMYO character. An SKU design referencing the POP MART × LABUBU pricing structure (RMB 59–99 / limited editions RMB 200–1,000+) is provided together. Cre8orClub and RATEL & PARTNERS jointly design the design, MD lineup, and pricing policy.

19-5. Scenario for the 12-episode short drama

A first design of the scenario for the 12-episode short drama, structured under 28 minutes per episode and under RMB 300,000, aligned with local regulations for short-form drama production. XOONY appears as the lead character, with OREER.C, Itaewon Pak, and MIMYO joining as supporting characters. PDK Music Label produces the OST in parallel.

19-7. Fan-pass QR system design

A QR-based fan-pass system design that manages SAGONG EE HO fandom enrollment, dwell, payment, and UGC activity in an integrated way. Minor data handling and data isolation structures are designed in line with PIPL standards.

19-8. AI labeling guide

A SAGONG EE HO IP Studio operating guide aligned with the AI-generated content labeling standards in China. It composes the labeling rules applied when SAGONG EE HO AI voice and AIGC content are exposed to the Chinese market.

19-9. Four-track KPI observation dashboard

A KPI observation dashboard across four tracks: Market, Commercial, IP Asset, and Studio Operation. RATEL & PARTNERS aggregates the data by channel on weekly, monthly, and quarterly cycles.

19-10. Phase 1 operating simulation memo

A simulation memo of the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio's operating flow from D-30 to D+90. It designs deliverable schedules by channel, the workflow among PDK Music Label, RATEL & PARTNERS, and Cre8orClub, and coordination points with MADverse execution resources.

19-11. Phase 2 entry decision criteria

A first design of the gate used after the D+90 review to consider Phase 2 entry. It designs the next-stage entry conditions, decision signals, and the decision-making structure.

19-12. 12 additional IP pipeline cards

Cards for 12 IPs that the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio will roll into the MAD POP C+C+C+X platform after SAGONG EE HO (see Part 6 Chapter 21 and Appendix A14).

Chapter 22

IP Studio Operations
An operating model anchored on one IP per year, five IPs over five years

Through the operation of SAGONG EE HO, the studio establishes 7 IP-development SOPs, a learning curve, and 3 new-IP discovery channels.

22-1. IP Development SOP 7 stages

The SAGONG EE HO IP Studio establishes the following IP-development SOPs through SAGONG EE HO operations.

  1. Character Design — design rules for a four-character multi-character structure
  2. World-building — the expandable structure of Cabinet 402 (캐비닛 402호) and the Diploma Universe (디프로마 유니버스)
  3. Music — application of the PDK Music Label K-Pop industrialization SOP
  4. OSMU — standardization of the 11-channel map
  5. Community — Cre8orClub fandom-building rules
  6. Data & Branding — integrated SOP combining with RATEL & PARTNERS
  7. Global Business — the licensing model under VP Lee Seung-gyu's leadership
22-2. Learning Curve SAGONG EE HO Phase 1 → Subsequent IPs

The operating data from SAGONG EE HO Phase 1 forms a learning curve that reduces the launch time and cost of subsequent IPs.

ItemSAGONG EE HO (Phase 1)Card #2 MIMYO (2026 Q4)Card #3 onward (2027~)
Launch preparation time90 daysCompressible (60 days)Further compressible (45 days)
First-wave deliverables14 itemsReuse of SAGONG EE HO assetsStandard-kit operation
Collaboration lines4 lines4 lines + learning curve4 lines + learning curve

As operating experience accumulates, the marginal cost of launching a new IP declines. This forms the basis for building the asset structure of an IP-studio company rather than a single-IP operating company.

22-3. New-IP Discovery Channels

New IPs are sourced through the following three channels.

  1. PDK Music Label Network — collaborative IP sourcing from Korea's pool of writers, performers, session players, and directors
  2. Nonuni Special Forces Entertainment In-House IP Incubation — development of expansion characters from the Cabinet 402 Diploma Universe
  3. Cre8orClub Creator Collaborations — co-development of IPs with external creators
Chapter 23

IP Lineup Value
within the C+C+C+X Platform

This chapter sets out the meaning of IP-lineup expansion, the distribution of the lineup across C+C+C+X, and the mapping for global expansion. The SAGONG EE HO IP Studio's IP lineup scales into a structure operating five IPs in parallel.

23-1. Meaning of IP-Lineup Expansion

SAGONG EE HO is the first execution reference of the MAD POP C+C+C+X platform. Once Card #2 MIMYO solo licensing, Card #3 Kim Hyung-suk composer IP, Card #4 XOONY short-form drama persona, and Card #5 OREER.C AI voice come online in sequence, the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio's lineup forms a structure operating five IPs in parallel. A stable IP-lineup-based content supply structure takes shape, and revenue lines accumulate together across all four areas.

23-2. Distribution of the Lineup within C+C+C+X

The following lays out how the IP lineup is distributed across C+C+C+X.

Business AreaFirst Seed IPSecond-wave Spin-off IPs
A. ContentSAGONG EE HO main rightsCard #3 Kim Hyung-suk composer IP, Card #5 OREER.C AI voice
B. CommunitySAGONG EE HO worldCard #4 XOONY dual persona (seasonal character within the world)
C. CommerceSAGONG EE HO concerts, collaborations, goodsCard #2 MIMYO solo licensing
D. ExchangeSAGONG EE HO copyrights, IP ABSCard #5 OREER.C AI voice licensing

This distribution explains how, within the C+C+C+X model, the SAGONG EE HO main rights serve as the first seed and five spin-off IPs progressively reinforce the revenue line on each axis.

23-3. Global Expansion Mapping Four-region sequence

Global expansion of the IP lineup is reviewed under the following four-region sequence.

SequenceRegionLead Line
1stChina (CN)MADverse execution resources + the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio's four lines
2ndKorea (KR)Nonuni Special Forces main rights + the Korean market
3rdSoutheast Asia (SEA)VP Lee Seung-gyu's global-business leadership + leveraging the Baby Shark track
4thEurope & U.S. (EU·US)UMG Universal Music + the Oxford ASMES line

For each sequence, the lines led by the SAGONG EE HO IP Studio and the lines launched jointly are designed differently. SAGONG EE HO is the lead IP of the first sequence (China), while Cards #2~#5 are the priority-deployment candidates for the second and third sequences.

A1. Full Text of the IP Bible's 12 Items
  1. Four-Character Profiles — Chinese-language profiles of OREER.C, XOONY, Itaewon Pak, and MIMYO
  2. Diploma Universe World-building — Chinese-language formulation of the "Digital from Analog" philosophy
  3. Cabinet 402 — Chinese-language exposition of the world-portal device and the rules for converting brand touchpoints
  4. Five Core Copy Lines — Korean-Chinese parallel versions, prepared under the principle of original-text preservation
  5. OSMU 11-Channel Map — Chinese-language formulation of the per-channel operating guide
  6. Tone & Manner Guide — tone rules for music, visuals, copy, and character utterances
  7. Expansion Rules — criteria for new characters, new channels, and new collaborations
  8. Collaboration Guide — per-industry collaboration rules and restrictions
  9. Fandom Operating Policy — fan-creation, UGC, licensing, and minor-protection rules
  10. Content Quality Standards — quality-review items for music, MV, short-form drama, and goods
  11. AI & AIGC Operating Guide — labeling and operating rules for AI voice and AIGC content
  12. Issue-Response Rules — operating guidance for negative exposure, shifts in market reception, and changes in the policy environment

RMB 300K~800K + 1~3%

b;eat · Seven Bräu

Streetwear and dance collaborations. Four-character goods bundled in. Streetwear, casual, and designer brands.

RMB 500K~1.5M + 3~5%

A11-1. Convenience-Store Industry LOI
  • Korea case: CU partnership (XOONY convenience-store part-timer prequel narrative)
  • China discussion targets: 4-5 convenience-store chains
  • Package proposal (subject to discussion): In-store BGM using new-track OSTs, MIMYO limited-edition goods package, and use of CU partnership case video
  • Initial pricing proposal for discussion: Fixed license RMB 300K~800K + revenue share 1~3%
A11-2. F&B Industry LOI
  • Korea case: b;eat robot-café partnership; Seven Bräu beer collaboration
  • China discussion targets: Café chains, F&B brands, and alcoholic-beverage and beverage brands
  • Package proposal (subject to discussion): Cabinet 402 themed beverages and desserts, MIMYO character cups and packaging, and bundled limited-edition goods
  • Initial pricing proposal for discussion: Reference benchmarks include Luckin × Moutai and HeyTea × FENDI (RMB 500K~2M to the IP side per collaboration)
A11-3. Fashion Industry LOI
  • Korea case: SAGONG EE HO collaboration track with Korean fashion brands
  • China discussion targets: Streetwear and casual brands; designer brands
  • Package proposal (subject to discussion): Itaewon Pak streetwear and dance collaboration; bundled four-character goods
  • Initial pricing proposal for discussion: Fixed license RMB 500K~1.5M + revenue share 3~5%
A11-4. Beauty Industry LOI
  • Korea case: Character-collaboration tracks in the Korean beauty market
  • China discussion targets: Color, fragrance, and skincare brands
  • Package proposal (subject to discussion): XOONY and MIMYO limited-edition character packaging; Cabinet 402 collection line
  • Initial pricing proposal for discussion: Fixed license RMB 800K~2M + revenue share 3~5%
A11-5. Household-Goods Industry LOI
  • Korea case: E-Mart benefit-style collaboration
  • China discussion targets: Stationery, accessories, home appliances, and accessory licensing
  • Package proposal (subject to discussion): MIMYO character licensing; four-character accessory line
  • Initial pricing proposal for discussion: MG RMB 100K~500K + 5~10% royalty on revenue
